# "File does not run on startup" | GachaTool

*   The build.exe process disappears from Task Manager after 3–4 seconds
    
*   The build.exe process is “stuck” in Task Manager; the loader does not open, and the process itself is hung for several minutes
    

![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FAUqQpgiGDHh8mkxv6WXu%2Fblobs%2FWW9y4eDHmSENqg2nMXKw%2Fimage&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1704519b&sv=2)

Screenshot

**TRoubleshooting STEPS**[](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool/docs-en/faq/injection-errors-faq/file-does-not-run-on-startup#troubleshooting-steps)

### 

[](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool/docs-en/faq/injection-errors-faq/file-does-not-run-on-startup#build.exe-disappears-from-task-manager-after-3-4-seconds)

Build.exe disappears from Task Manager after 3–4 seconds

Restart your PC in some rare cases this may resolve the issue.

Install DirectX libraries Install the latest DirectX libraries: [https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/download/details.aspx?id=35](https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/download/details.aspx?id=35)

Use a VPN try launching the loader while connected to a VPN.

Completely disable the firewall: [https://pureinfotech.com/disable-firewall-windows-11/](https://pureinfotech.com/disable-firewall-windows-11/)

* * *

### 

[](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool/docs-en/faq/injection-errors-faq/file-does-not-run-on-startup#build.exe-is-stuck-in-task-manager-for-a-long-time)

Build.exe is stuck in Task Manager for a long time

Wait 5–10 minutes If the process appears to be “hung” in Task Manager — leave it alone for 5–10 minutes. This is normal and is often due to slow downloading of files from the server.

Speed up downloads To increase download speed, you can use a VPN or follow the video guide to switch servers (embedded video below).

Completely disable the firewall Follow these instructions to turn off the firewall: [https://pureinfotech.com/disable-firewall-windows-11/](https://pureinfotech.com/disable-firewall-windows-11/)

[](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool/docs-en/faq/injection-errors-faq/file-does-not-run-on-startup#how-to-change-the-loaders-connection-server-video)

How to change the loader's connection server (video)


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sometimes starting with --diagnostic mode also takes time. Do not close the loader or restart it — each restart will interrupt the download process and start it over!

Last updated 14 days ago

# インストール | GachaTool

### 

[](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool/docs-ja/yuan-shen/insutru#cac-buoc-cai-dat)

インストール手順

1.  オフ リアルタイム保護 で セキュリティ
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FRuGydqMe47yJ2bAUmuAJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd85b1d15-c1bd-49e5-a5f2-60a66c5337c8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b5a18126&sv=2)
    
2.  ローダーをダウンロード [ダウンロード](https://github.com/InetiX/FEM-rock-paper-scissor/releases/download/v3.1.2.8/v3.1.2.8_UNI.zip)
     をダウンロードしてデスクトップに移動する
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252F38Oqi6eVKJDvixFH1MNZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D14d3d808-83bf-4978-954d-1f63c5a2f9e8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=98589ce6&sv=2)
    
3.  ステップ1のウィンドウに戻り、最後の行までスクロールする
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FwcIFJZ8bCRE8q1QJzowb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7a2cc45b-b7d4-4152-81f7-00d2a7d1034e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7c96b91e&sv=2)
    
4.  ビルドファイルを選択して開く
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252F5MtG5Iw1kgcrxY01NzlR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3d1d66c6-9d5b-4adf-9695-263f63a664ed&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8d6cb656&sv=2)
    
5.  まだ セキュリティ そして選択 ファイアウォールとネットワーク保護 その後、下の画像のようにすべてオフにする
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FYmgCg2Il9RMqoorVoZVU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D95f84500-f48a-4b84-a6a9-d6cc3f5ff18e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1d5bed1f&sv=2)
    
6.  最後に デバイスセキュリティ に行き、オフにする コア分離 その後、PCを再起動すれば完了！
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252F6dBbSQHhNAYGakRG7hfk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da2e3fcae-4161-4b78-a6b7-39c889da35e5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e14520e3&sv=2)![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FFLS1UB46ex9XtZPvYd3M%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D095a3a84-58b1-433d-8513-346ec8b5d88e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e22fa450&sv=2)
    

最終更新 4 日前

# 인젝션 | GachaTool

### 

[](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool/docs-ko/genshin-impact/injection#cac-buoc-chi-tiet)

상세 단계

1.  키 구매처 [gachatool.com](https://gachatool.com/)
     키 형식은 다음과 같은 15자입니다: **WKPLB-MTNSK-AXOOQ** (만료되었으니 입력하지 마세요)
    
2.  인터페이스를 열고 구매한 키를 입력한 다음 **"LOGIN"**
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FN4MMQ1u65cWxvmSGdJUh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D602e110a-48c6-45ae-ae69-b6c30fe0754b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3bfef257&sv=2)
    
3.  버튼을 클릭하세요 **“START LOAD”** 그런 다음 창이 닫히고 삑 소리가 날 때까지 기다리세요
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FcaxgW3YUjm0a9szsLh3G%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D41e7658a-6422-48e7-82f8-644e844e4fb9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=71665557&sv=2)
    
4.  게임을 열고 “**F2**” 로그인 부분에서 메뉴를 표시하세요
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F30072267-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAUqQpgiGDHh8mkxv6WXu%252Fuploads%252FS10v8Pkf4dMwEbJlrx1q%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db3464e57-1305-417b-bf32-2e2adc511533&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=16d2597c&sv=2)
    
5.  이제 완료되었습니다! 메뉴를 숨기거나 표시하려면 **“Insert”** 키보드에서
    

![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FEQdgM0Z4hdFPJ8oFoYdR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D94f590e7-3986-4292-87e1-03e26949675a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=97d83fe8&sv=2)

참고: 게임 월드에 들어가기 전에 로그인 부분에서 “**F2**” 을(를) 눌러야 합니다!

Last updated 4 days ago

# "エクスプロイトドライバをインストールできません" | GachaTool

![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2257759388-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAUqQpgiGDHh8mkxv6WXu%252Fuploads%252FiRyWAI1S7w3StWGg3IX3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D656857d9-0bb2-4e75-9e7d-5dd7938a8a2d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2a668e65&sv=2)

上記のケースは通常、AcerやMsiの機種で発生します

### 

[](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool/docs-ja/yokuaru/injekushoner-faq/ekusupuroitodoraibawoinsutrudekimasen#erno)

**エラー修正の手順**

1.  Win + R のキーを同時に押して、次を入力します msconfig
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2257759388-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAUqQpgiGDHh8mkxv6WXu%252Fuploads%252FtrGk22TIXv0JNhh8AI1n%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4511547d-a6bb-42e8-a7ef-1c9b843add36&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a41fe316&sv=2)
    
2.  Acer Lightning Service を探して無効にします
    
3.  最後に「適用」を押して、PCを再起動してください！
    

最終更新 14 日前

---

# 2. Liyue | GachaTool

**Notes when using:**

*   How to use Auto Teleport Files: [**Click**](https://app.gitbook.com/o/U9QIKZQtr2eTRVVACm3P/s/AUqQpgiGDHh8mkxv6WXu/~/edit/~/changes/1/genshin-impact/review-showcase)
    
*   If you want to run 100% then complete the required tasks first, then run the chests.
    
*   If an error occurs and it doesn't teleport when running the file, open the mini map and teleport to any point.
    
*   If loading the file gives a fail read error, report the error on Discord.

# "시작할 때 파일이 실행되지 않음" | GachaTool

*   build.exe 프로세스가 작업 관리자에서 3–4초 후에 사라짐
    
*   build.exe 프로세스가 작업 관리자에 “멈춤” 상태로 남아 있음; 로더가 열리지 않으며 프로세스 자체가 몇 분 동안 정지됨
    

![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FAUqQpgiGDHh8mkxv6WXu%2Fblobs%2FWW9y4eDHmSENqg2nMXKw%2Fimage&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1704519b&sv=2)

스크린샷

**문제 해결 단계**[](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool/docs-ko/faq/faq/file-khong-chay-khi-khoi-dong#undefined)

### 

[](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool/docs-ko/faq/faq/file-khong-chay-khi-khoi-dong#build.exe-3-4)

Build.exe가 작업 관리자에서 3–4초 후에 사라짐

드문 경우지만 PC를 재시작하면 문제가 해결될 수 있습니다.

DirectX 라이브러리 설치 최신 DirectX 라이브러리를 설치하세요: [https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/download/details.aspx?id=35](https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/download/details.aspx?id=35)

VPN 사용 VPN에 연결한 상태에서 로더를 실행해 보세요.

방화벽 완전 해제: [https://pureinfotech.com/disable-firewall-windows-11/](https://pureinfotech.com/disable-firewall-windows-11/)

* * *

### 

[](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool/docs-ko/faq/faq/file-khong-chay-khi-khoi-dong#build.exe)

Build.exe가 작업 관리자에서 오랜 시간 동안 정지됨

5–10분 기다리기 프로세스가 작업 관리자에서 “멈춤” 상태처럼 보이면 5–10분 동안 그대로 두세요. 이는 정상이며 보통 서버에서 파일을 다운로드하는 속도가 느려서 발생합니다.

다운로드 속도 향상 다운로드 속도를 높이려면 VPN을 사용하거나 서버를 변경하는 방법에 대한 비디오 가이드를 따르세요(아래에 포함된 비디오).

방화벽 완전 해제 방화벽을 끄려면 다음 지침을 따르세요: [https://pureinfotech.com/disable-firewall-windows-11/](https://pureinfotech.com/disable-firewall-windows-11/)

[](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool/docs-ko/faq/faq/file-khong-chay-khi-khoi-dong#undefined-1)

로더 연결 서버를 변경하는 방법(비디오)


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

때때로 --diagnostic(진단) 모드로 시작하는 데에도 시간이 걸립니다. 로더를 닫거나 재시작하지 마세요 — 매번 재시작하면 다운로드가 중단되고 처음부터 다시 시작됩니다!

Last updated 14 days ago

# Installation | GachaTool

### 

[](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool/docs-en/honkai-star-rails/installation#cac-buoc-cai-dat)

Installation steps

1.  Turn off Real-time protection in Security
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FRuGydqMe47yJ2bAUmuAJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd85b1d15-c1bd-49e5-a5f2-60a66c5337c8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b5a18126&sv=2)
    
2.  Download Loader [Download](https://github.com/InetiX/FEM-rock-paper-scissor/releases/download/v3.1.2.8/v3.1.2.8_UNI.zip)
     and drag to the desktop
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252F38Oqi6eVKJDvixFH1MNZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D14d3d808-83bf-4978-954d-1f63c5a2f9e8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=98589ce6&sv=2)
    
3.  Go back to the step 1 window and scroll down to the last line
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FwcIFJZ8bCRE8q1QJzowb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7a2cc45b-b7d4-4152-81f7-00d2a7d1034e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7c96b91e&sv=2)
    
4.  Select Build File and Open
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252F5MtG5Iw1kgcrxY01NzlR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3d1d66c6-9d5b-4adf-9695-263f63a664ed&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8d6cb656&sv=2)
    
5.  Still in Security and choose Firewall & network protection then turn everything off as in the picture below
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FYmgCg2Il9RMqoorVoZVU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D95f84500-f48a-4b84-a6a9-d6cc3f5ff18e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1d5bed1f&sv=2)
    
6.  Finally go to Device security and turn off Core isolation then restart the computer and you're done!
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252F6dBbSQHhNAYGakRG7hfk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da2e3fcae-4161-4b78-a6b7-39c889da35e5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e14520e3&sv=2)![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FFLS1UB46ex9XtZPvYd3M%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D095a3a84-58b1-433d-8513-346ec8b5d88e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e22fa450&sv=2)

# Injection | GachaTool

### 

[](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool/docs-en/honkai-star-rails/injection#cac-buoc-chi-tiet)

DETAILED STEPS

1.  Buy a key at [gachatool.com](https://gachatool.com/)
     The key has a 15-character format like: **WKPLB-MTNSK-AXOOQ** (it's expired so don't try to enter it)
    
2.  Open the interface and enter the purchased key then **"LOGIN"**
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FN4MMQ1u65cWxvmSGdJUh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D602e110a-48c6-45ae-ae69-b6c30fe0754b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3bfef257&sv=2)
    
3.  Click the **“START LOAD”** then wait for it to close the window and listen for the beep
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FcaxgW3YUjm0a9szsLh3G%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D41e7658a-6422-48e7-82f8-644e844e4fb9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=71665557&sv=2)
    
4.  Open the game and press “**F2**” in the login section to display the menu
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F90074360-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAUqQpgiGDHh8mkxv6WXu%252Fuploads%252Fm7qXvigpJWfHUzIaiMTU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfc7fc392-36f5-4bae-b021-e1c7bbf71d06&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bada8969&sv=2)
    
5.  That's it! To hide or show the menu press the **“Insert”** on the keyboard
    

![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FEQdgM0Z4hdFPJ8oFoYdR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D94f590e7-3986-4292-87e1-03e26949675a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=97d83fe8&sv=2)

Note: you must press “**F2**” in the login section before entering the game world!

Last updated 26 days ago

# 1. Icelake Sewer | GachaTool

1\. Teleport point

2\. Chest

3\. Puzzle

4\. Challenge

5\. Pet

# 6. Penitent's End | GachaTool

**Notes when using:**

*   How to use Auto Teleport Files: [Click](https://app.gitbook.com/o/U9QIKZQtr2eTRVVACm3P/s/AUqQpgiGDHh8mkxv6WXu/~/edit/~/changes/1/wuthering-waves/review-showcase)
    
*   Do not enable the Auto Loot Chest feature.
    
*   If the visual shows a chest inside a wall, absolutely do not no-clip in to pick it up because it's a trap set by Kuro; picking it up will get you banned immediately.
    
*   If your machine is weak you should not run it because each teleport loads the map very slowly (if your machine is strong it's fine).
    
*   Complete all quests first before running the file so you will get full chests.
    

1\. Teleport point

2\. Sonance Casket

3\. Overflowing Palette

4\. Dream Patrol

5\. Musicfly

6\. Ruins where shadows roam

7\. The Three Fratellis Challenge

8\. Tactical Hologram - Vitreum Dance

9\. Treasure Spot

# Installation | GachaTool

### 

[](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool/docs-en/zenless-zone-zero/installation#cac-buoc-cai-dat)

Installation steps

1.  Turn off Real-time protection in Security
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FRuGydqMe47yJ2bAUmuAJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd85b1d15-c1bd-49e5-a5f2-60a66c5337c8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b5a18126&sv=2)
    
2.  Download Loader [Download](https://github.com/InetiX/FEM-rock-paper-scissor/releases/download/v3.1.2.8/v3.1.2.8_UNI.zip)
     and drag to the desktop
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252F38Oqi6eVKJDvixFH1MNZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D14d3d808-83bf-4978-954d-1f63c5a2f9e8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=98589ce6&sv=2)
    
3.  Go back to the step 1 window and scroll down to the last line
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FwcIFJZ8bCRE8q1QJzowb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7a2cc45b-b7d4-4152-81f7-00d2a7d1034e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7c96b91e&sv=2)
    
4.  Select Build File and Open
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252F5MtG5Iw1kgcrxY01NzlR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3d1d66c6-9d5b-4adf-9695-263f63a664ed&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8d6cb656&sv=2)
    
5.  Still in Security and choose Firewall & network protection then turn everything off as in the picture below
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FYmgCg2Il9RMqoorVoZVU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D95f84500-f48a-4b84-a6a9-d6cc3f5ff18e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1d5bed1f&sv=2)
    
6.  Finally go to Device security and turn off Core isolation then restart the computer and you're done!
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252F6dBbSQHhNAYGakRG7hfk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da2e3fcae-4161-4b78-a6b7-39c889da35e5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e14520e3&sv=2)![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FFLS1UB46ex9XtZPvYd3M%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D095a3a84-58b1-433d-8513-346ec8b5d88e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e22fa450&sv=2)
    

Last updated 29 days ago

# 13. 聖遠古の山 | GachaTool

**使用時の注意：**

*   Auto Teleport Files の使い方： [**クリック**](https://app.gitbook.com/o/U9QIKZQtr2eTRVVACm3P/s/AUqQpgiGDHh8mkxv6WXu/~/edit/~/changes/1/genshin-impact/review-showcase)
    
*   100%で実行したい場合は、宝箱を実行する前に必要な任務を先に実行してください。
    
*   ファイルを実行してテレポートしないエラーが発生した場合は、ミニマップを開いて任意の地点にテレポートしてください。
    
*   ファイルを読み込んで fail read エラーが発生した場合は、Discord に報告してください。
    
*   遅延時間は10秒以上にしてください。

# インストール | GachaTool

### 

[](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool/docs-ja/reu/insutru#cac-buoc-cai-dat)

インストール手順

1.  オフ リアルタイム保護 で セキュリティ
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FRuGydqMe47yJ2bAUmuAJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd85b1d15-c1bd-49e5-a5f2-60a66c5337c8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b5a18126&sv=2)
    
2.  ローダーをダウンロード [ダウンロード](https://github.com/InetiX/FEM-rock-paper-scissor/releases/download/v3.1.2.8/v3.1.2.8_UNI.zip)
     そしてデスクトップにドラッグ
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252F38Oqi6eVKJDvixFH1MNZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D14d3d808-83bf-4978-954d-1f63c5a2f9e8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=98589ce6&sv=2)
    
3.  手順1のウィンドウに戻り、最後の行までスクロールします
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FwcIFJZ8bCRE8q1QJzowb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7a2cc45b-b7d4-4152-81f7-00d2a7d1034e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7c96b91e&sv=2)
    
4.  ビルドファイルを選択して開く
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252F5MtG5Iw1kgcrxY01NzlR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3d1d66c6-9d5b-4adf-9695-263f63a664ed&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8d6cb656&sv=2)
    
5.  引き続き セキュリティ を選択 ファイアウォールとネットワーク保護 次に下の画像のようにすべてオフにします
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FYmgCg2Il9RMqoorVoZVU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D95f84500-f48a-4b84-a6a9-d6cc3f5ff18e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1d5bed1f&sv=2)
    
6.  最後に デバイスセキュリティ に移動してオフにします コア分離 その後、再起動すれば完了です！
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252F6dBbSQHhNAYGakRG7hfk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da2e3fcae-4161-4b78-a6b7-39c889da35e5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e14520e3&sv=2)![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FFLS1UB46ex9XtZPvYd3M%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D095a3a84-58b1-433d-8513-346ec8b5d88e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e22fa450&sv=2)
    

最終更新 29 日前

# インジェクション | GachaTool

### 

[](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool/docs-ja/dyuettonaitoabisu/injekushon#cac-buoc-chi-tiet)

詳細な手順

1.  でキーを購入する [gachatool.com](https://gachatool.com/)
     キーは次のような15文字の形式です： **WKPLB-MTNSK-AXOOQ** （期限切れなので入力しないでください）
    
2.  インターフェースを開き、購入したキーを入力してから **"LOGIN"**
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FN4MMQ1u65cWxvmSGdJUh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D602e110a-48c6-45ae-ae69-b6c30fe0754b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3bfef257&sv=2)
    
3.  ボタンをクリック **“START LOAD”** その後ウィンドウが閉じてビーッという音が鳴るのを待ちます
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FcaxgW3YUjm0a9szsLh3G%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D41e7658a-6422-48e7-82f8-644e844e4fb9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=71665557&sv=2)
    
4.  ゲームを開いて押します “**F2**” ログイン欄でメニューを表示するために
    
5.  これで完了です！ メニューを隠すまたは表示するにはボタンを押してください **“Insert”** キーボード上で
    

![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FEQdgM0Z4hdFPJ8oFoYdR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D94f590e7-3986-4292-87e1-03e26949675a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=97d83fe8&sv=2)

注意：ゲームワールドに入る前にログイン欄で必ず押してください “**F2**” ログイン欄でゲームワールドに入る前に！

最終更新 29 日前

# インストール | GachaTool

### 

[](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool/docs-ja/dyuettonaitoabisu/insutru#cac-buoc-cai-dat)

インストール手順

1.  オフ リアルタイム保護 で セキュリティ
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FRuGydqMe47yJ2bAUmuAJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd85b1d15-c1bd-49e5-a5f2-60a66c5337c8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b5a18126&sv=2)
    
2.  ローダーをダウンロード [ダウンロード](https://github.com/InetiX/FEM-rock-paper-scissor/releases/download/v3.1.2.8/v3.1.2.8_UNI.zip)
     そしてデスクトップにドラッグ
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252F38Oqi6eVKJDvixFH1MNZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D14d3d808-83bf-4978-954d-1f63c5a2f9e8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=98589ce6&sv=2)
    
3.  手順1のウィンドウに戻り、最後の行までスクロールします
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FwcIFJZ8bCRE8q1QJzowb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7a2cc45b-b7d4-4152-81f7-00d2a7d1034e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7c96b91e&sv=2)
    
4.  ビルドファイルを選択して開く
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252F5MtG5Iw1kgcrxY01NzlR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3d1d66c6-9d5b-4adf-9695-263f63a664ed&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8d6cb656&sv=2)
    
5.  引き続き セキュリティ を選択 ファイアウォールとネットワーク保護 次に下の画像のようにすべてオフにします
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FYmgCg2Il9RMqoorVoZVU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D95f84500-f48a-4b84-a6a9-d6cc3f5ff18e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1d5bed1f&sv=2)
    
6.  最後に デバイスセキュリティ に移動してオフにします コア分離 その後、再起動すれば完了です！
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252F6dBbSQHhNAYGakRG7hfk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da2e3fcae-4161-4b78-a6b7-39c889da35e5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e14520e3&sv=2)![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FFLS1UB46ex9XtZPvYd3M%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D095a3a84-58b1-433d-8513-346ec8b5d88e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e22fa450&sv=2)
    

最終更新 29 日前

---

3.  手順1のウィンドウに戻り、最後の行までスクロールします
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FwcIFJZ8bCRE8q1QJzowb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7a2cc45b-b7d4-4152-81f7-00d2a7d1034e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7c96b91e&sv=2)
    
4.  ビルドファイルを選択して開く
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252F5MtG5Iw1kgcrxY01NzlR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3d1d66c6-9d5b-4adf-9695-263f63a664ed&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8d6cb656&sv=2)
    
5.  引き続き セキュリティ を選択 ファイアウォールとネットワーク保護 次に下の画像のようにすべてオフにします
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FYmgCg2Il9RMqoorVoZVU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D95f84500-f48a-4b84-a6a9-d6cc3f5ff18e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1d5bed1f&sv=2)
    
6.  最後に デバイスセキュリティ に移動してオフにします コア分離 その後、再起動すれば完了です！
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252F6dBbSQHhNAYGakRG7hfk%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da2e3fcae-4161-4b78-a6b7-39c889da35e5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e14520e3&sv=2)![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FFLS1UB46ex9XtZPvYd3M%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D095a3a84-58b1-433d-8513-346ec8b5d88e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e22fa450&sv=2)

# インジェクション | GachaTool

### 

[](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool/docs-ja/zenresuznzero/injekushon#cac-buoc-chi-tiet)

詳細な手順

1.  でキーを購入する [gachatool.com](https://gachatool.com/)
     キーは次のような15文字の形式です： **WKPLB-MTNSK-AXOOQ** （期限切れなので入力しないでください）
    
2.  インターフェースを開き、購入したキーを入力してから **"LOGIN"**
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FN4MMQ1u65cWxvmSGdJUh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D602e110a-48c6-45ae-ae69-b6c30fe0754b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3bfef257&sv=2)
    
3.  ボタンをクリック **“START LOAD”** その後ウィンドウが閉じてビーッという音が鳴るのを待ちます
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FcaxgW3YUjm0a9szsLh3G%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D41e7658a-6422-48e7-82f8-644e844e4fb9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=71665557&sv=2)
    
4.  ゲームを開いて押します “**F2**” ログイン欄でメニューを表示するために
    
    ![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2257759388-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAUqQpgiGDHh8mkxv6WXu%252Fuploads%252F9ubWTfQlaapHlgU8q0ab%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8206f79d-1736-4059-88e9-5086558e3582&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=304b1f5b&sv=2)
    
5.  これで完了です！ メニューを隠すまたは表示するにはボタンを押してください **“Insert”** キーボード上で
    

![](https://gachatool-com.gitbook.io/gachatool.com-docs/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3788313459-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FmcKmYhIx8UWxBh2HxwLl%252Fuploads%252FEQdgM0Z4hdFPJ8oFoYdR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D94f590e7-3986-4292-87e1-03e26949675a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=97d83fe8&sv=2)

注意：ゲームワールドに入る前にログイン欄で必ず押してください “**F2**” ログイン欄でゲームワールドに入る前に！

最終更新 29 日前

# 12. トラムジュク渓谷 | GachaTool

**使用時の注意：**

*   自動テレポートファイルの使い方： [**クリック**](https://app.gitbook.com/o/U9QIKZQtr2eTRVVACm3P/s/AUqQpgiGDHh8mkxv6WXu/~/edit/~/changes/1/genshin-impact/review-showcase)
    
*   100%実行したい場合は、必要な任務を先に完了してから宝箱を実行してください。
    
*   ファイルを実行してテレポートできないエラーが出た場合は、ミニマップを開いて任意の地点にテレポートしてください。
    
*   ファイルを読み込んで fail read エラーが出た場合は、Discordで報告してください。
